> Analyze them against science

â— learning-sciences-researcher(Analyze docs against learning science)
  â¿ Â Done (5 tool uses Â· 34.1k tokens Â· 1m 46s)

â— Brutal analysis. Key issues:

  False Precision
  - Arbitrary weights (30% decay, 25% centrality) presented as research
  - Thresholds (90% retention, 85% procedural) lack citations
  - NCDE decision tree oversimplifies complex cognition

  Terminology Misuse
  - "Z-Score" isn't a z-score
  - "Stability" redefined from its research meaning
  - Could mislead readers

  Missing Science
  - Sleep consolidation
  - Individual differences
  - Testing effect (underplayed)
  - Affective/motivational factors
  - Dual coding, elaboration, generation effects

  War Mode Problem
  - Legitimizes cramming despite spacing effect research
  - Should have stronger warnings

  Recommendations
  1. Add actual citations
  2. Say "we chose X" not "research shows X" for design decisions
  3. Add uncertainty language
  4. Address individual variation
  5. Warn more strongly about cramming modes

  Want me to have the docarchitect fix these issues in the docs?

     Plan: Cortex Start UX Improvements

     Problem Statement

     User reported that cortex start:
     1. Shows random Parsons from random modules instead of prioritizing their declared struggle areas
     2. No progress dashboard shown before session starts
     3. Struggle sections from struggles.yaml are not being used

     Root Cause Analysis

     Current Flow (cortex start)

     cortex_start() -> CortexSession(modules, limit) -> load_queue()
                                                           |
                                                    get_adaptive_session()  <-- Problem here
                                                           |
                                                    Orders by FSRS due_date only

     What Exists But Is Not Connected:

     - struggles.yaml - Well-defined struggle areas with chains, severity, sections
     - struggle_weights table (migration 015) - Has schema for priorities
     - v_struggle_priority view - Priority formula: struggle_weight*3 + ncde_weight*2 + (1-retrievability)
     - create_struggle_heatmap() in cortex_visuals.py - Dashboard component exists

     What's Missing:

     1. Import: struggles.yaml -> struggle_weights table
     2. Query: get_adaptive_session() doesn't query v_struggle_priority
     3. Dashboard: No progress display before session starts
     4. Default behavior: Should prioritize struggles, not just FSRS due dates

     Implementation Plan

     Phase 1: Import Struggles from YAML to Database

     File: src/cli/cortex.py

     Add command:
     @cortex_app.command("struggles")
     def cortex_struggles(
         import_yaml: bool = typer.Option(False, "--import", help="Import from struggles.yaml"),
         show: bool = typer.Option(True, "--show", help="Show current struggle weights"),
     ):
         """Manage struggle weights for prioritized study."""

     Implementation:
     - Parse struggles.yaml using PyYAML
     - Insert/update struggle_weights table with module/section/severity/failure_modes
     - Show heatmap of current struggle weights

     Phase 2: Add Progress Dashboard Before Session

     Files:
     - src/cli/cortex.py (add dashboard display)
     - src/delivery/cortex_visuals.py (may need tweaks)

     Before session.run(), display:
     +------------------------------------------+
     |       CORTEX - NEURAL STUDY HUB          |
     +------------------------------------------+
     | Overall Mastery: 42%  |  Streak: 7 days  |
     +------------------------------------------+
     | STRUGGLE ZONES (Priority Order)          |
     | [!] Module 5: Ethernet/Switching  12%    |
     | [!] Module 8: IPv4 Subnetting     23%    |
     | [*] Module 9: ARP/ND              45%    |
     +------------------------------------------+
     | Today's Session: 20 atoms                |
     | - 8 from struggle zones                  |
     | - 7 FSRS due reviews                     |
     | - 5 new material                         |
     +------------------------------------------+
     Press ENTER to start or 'c' to configure...

     Phase 3: Modify get_adaptive_session() to Use Struggle Priority

     File: src/study/study_service.py

     Change query to use v_struggle_priority view:

     def get_adaptive_session(
         self,
         limit: int = 20,
         include_new: bool = True,
         interleave: bool = True,
         use_struggles: bool = True,  # NEW parameter
     ) -> list[dict]:
         """Get atoms prioritized by struggle weights + FSRS."""

         if use_struggles:
             # Use v_struggle_priority view for ordering
             query = """
                 SELECT vsp.*, 'struggle' as source
                 FROM v_struggle_priority vsp
                 WHERE vsp.atom_type IN ('mcq', 'true_false', 'parsons', 'matching')
                 ORDER BY vsp.priority_score DESC
                 LIMIT :limit
             """
         else:
             # Original FSRS-only ordering
             ...

     Phase 4: Wire Up cortex start to Show Dashboard + Use Struggles

     File: src/cli/cortex.py

     Modify cortex_start():
     @cortex_app.command("start")
     def cortex_start(...):
         # 1. Load struggle weights if not populated
         _ensure_struggles_imported()

         # 2. Show progress dashboard
         _show_pre_session_dashboard()

         # 3. Start session with struggle-prioritized atoms
         session = CortexSession(modules=module_list, limit=limit, war_mode=war_mode)
         session.run()

     Files to Modify

     | File                           | Changes                                                                               |
     |--------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
     | src/cli/cortex.py              | Add struggles command, add dashboard before session, add _ensure_struggles_imported() |
     | src/study/study_service.py     | Modify get_adaptive_session() to query v_struggle_priority                            |
     | src/delivery/cortex_visuals.py | Possibly add create_pre_session_dashboard() panel                                     |

     Order of Implementation

     1. Add struggles command - import YAML to DB

       2172 +  def _load_struggles_yaml() -> dict:
       2173 +      """Load struggles.yaml from project root."""
       2174 +      project_root = Path(__file__).parent.parent.parent
       2175 +      yaml_path = project_root / "struggles.yaml"
       2176 +      if not yaml_path.exists():
       2177 +          return {}
       2178 +      with open(yaml_path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
       2179 +          return yaml.safe_load(f) or {}
       2180 +

       2182 +  def _import_struggles_to_db() -> dict:
       2183 +      """
       2184 +      Import struggles from struggles.yaml into struggle_weights table.
       2185 +
       2186 +      Returns dict with import stats.
       2187 +      """
       2188 +      data = _load_struggles_yaml()
       2189 +      if not data or "struggles" not in data:
       2190 +          return {"imported": 0, "error": "No struggles found in struggles.yaml"}
       2191 +
       2192 +      struggles = data["struggles"]
       2193 +      severity_to_weight = {
       2194 +          "critical": 1.0,
       2195 +          "high": 0.75,
       2196 +          "medium": 0.5,
       2197 +          "low": 0.25,
       2198 +      }
       2199 +
       2200 +      imported = 0
       2201 +      errors = []
       2202 +
       2203 +      with engine.connect() as conn:
       2204 +          for struggle in struggles:
       2205 +              module = struggle.get("module")
       2206 +              if not module:
       2207 +                  continue
       2208 +
       2209 +              severity = struggle.get("severity", "medium")
       2210 +              weight = severity_to_weight.get(severity, 0.5)
       2211 +              failure_modes = struggle.get("failure_modes", [])
       2212 +              notes = struggle.get("notes", "")
       2213 +              sections = struggle.get("sections", [])
       2214 +
       2215 +              try:
       2216 +                  # Insert module-level weight
       2217 +                  conn.execute(
       2218 +                      text("""
       2219 +                          INSERT INTO struggle_weights
       2220 +                              (module_number, section_id, severity, weight, failure_modes, notes)
       2221 +                          VALUES
       2222 +                              (:module, NULL, :severity, :weight, :failure_modes, :notes)
       2223 +                          ON CONFLICT (module_number, section_id)
       2224 +                          DO UPDATE SET
       2225 +                              severity = EXCLUDED.severity,
       2226 +                              weight = EXCLUDED.weight,
       2227 +                              failure_modes = EXCLUDED.failure_modes,
       2228 +                              notes = EXCLUDED.notes,
       2229 +                              updated_at = NOW()
       2230 +                      """),
       2231 +                      {
       2232 +                          "module": module,
       2233 +                          "severity": severity,
       2234 +                          "weight": weight,
       2235 +                          "failure_modes": failure_modes or [],
       2236 +                          "notes": notes,
       2237 +                      }
       2238 +                  )
       2239 +                  imported += 1
       2240 +
       2241 +                  # Also insert section-level weights if specified
       2242 +                  for section_id in sections:
       2243 +                      conn.execute(
       2244 +                          text("""
       2245 +                              INSERT INTO struggle_weights
       2246 +                                  (module_number, section_id, severity, weight, failure_modes, notes)
       2247 +                              VALUES
       2248 +                                  (:module, :section_id, :severity, :weight, :failure_modes, :notes)
       2249 +                              ON CONFLICT (module_number, section_id)
       2250 +                              DO UPDATE SET
       2251 +                                  severity = EXCLUDED.severity,
       2252 +                                  weight = EXCLUDED.weight,
       2253 +                                  failure_modes = EXCLUDED.failure_modes,
       2254 +                                  notes = EXCLUDED.notes,
       2255 +                                  updated_at = NOW()
       2256 +                          """),
       2257 +                          {
       2258 +                              "module": module,
       2259 +                              "section_id": str(section_id),
       2260 +                              "severity": severity,
       2261 +                              "weight": weight,
       2262 +                              "failure_modes": failure_modes or [],
       2263 +                              "notes": notes,
       2264 +                          }
       2265 +                      )
       2266 +                      imported += 1
       2267 +
       2268 +              except Exception as e:
       2269 +                  errors.append(f"Module {module}: {e}")
       2270 +
       2271 +          conn.commit()
       2272 +
       2273 +      return {"imported": imported, "errors": errors}

       2276 +  def _get_struggle_stats() -> list[dict]:
       2277 +      """Get current struggle weights from database with mastery info."""
       2278 +      with engine.connect() as conn:
       2279 +          result = conn.execute(
       2280 +              text("""
       2281 +                  SELECT
       2282 +                      sw.module_number,
       2283 +                      sw.severity,
       2284 +                      sw.weight,
       2285 +                      sw.notes,
       2286 +                      COALESCE(AVG(csm.mastery_score), 0) as avg_mastery,
       2287 +                      COUNT(DISTINCT la.id) as atom_count
       2288 +                  FROM struggle_weights sw
       2289 +                  LEFT JOIN ccna_sections cs ON cs.module_number = sw.module_number
       2290 +                  LEFT JOIN ccna_section_mastery csm ON csm.section_id = cs.section_id
       2291 +                  LEFT JOIN learning_atoms la ON la.ccna_section_id = cs.section_id
       2292 +                  WHERE sw.section_id IS NULL  -- Module-level only
       2293 +                  GROUP BY sw.module_number, sw.severity, sw.weight, sw.notes
       2294 +                  ORDER BY sw.weight DESC, sw.module_number
       2295 +              """)
       2296 +          )
       2297 +          return [dict(row._mapping) for row in result.fetchall()]
       2298 +
       2299 +
       2300 +  def _get_pre_session_stats() -> dict:
       2301 +      """Get stats for pre-session dashboard."""
       2302 +      with engine.connect() as conn:
       2303 +          # Overall mastery
       2304 +          mastery_result = conn.execute(
       2305 +              text("""
       2306 +                  SELECT
       2307 +                      AVG(mastery_score) as overall_mastery,
       2308 +                      COUNT(*) as sections_total,
       2309 +                      COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE is_completed) as sections_complete
       2310 +                  FROM ccna_section_mastery
       2311 +                  WHERE user_id = 'default'
       2312 +              """)
       2313 +          )
       2314 +          mastery_row = mastery_result.fetchone()
       2315 +
       2316 +          # Streak days (simplified)
       2317 +          streak_result = conn.execute(
       2318 +              text("""
       2319 +                  SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT DATE(responded_at)) as streak
       2320 +                  FROM atom_responses
       2321 +                  WHERE responded_at >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL '30 days'
       2322 +              """)
       2323 +          )
       2324 +          streak_row = streak_result.fetchone()
       2325 +
       2326 +          # Struggle zone stats using v_struggle_priority
       2327 +          struggle_result = conn.execute(
       2328 +              text("""
       2329 +                  SELECT
       2330 +                      module_number,
       2331 +                      COUNT(*) as atom_count,
       2332 +                      AVG(priority_score) as avg_priority
       2333 +                  FROM v_struggle_priority
       2334 +                  WHERE struggle_weight >= 0.5  -- Only significant struggles
       2335 +                  GROUP BY module_number
       2336 +                  ORDER BY avg_priority DESC
       2337 +                  LIMIT 5
       2338 +              """)
       2339 +          )
       2340 +          struggle_zones = [dict(row._mapping) for row in struggle_result.fetchall()]
       2341 +
       2342 +          # Session composition preview
       2343 +          session_result = conn.execute(
       2344 +              text("""
       2345 +                  WITH struggle_atoms AS (
       2346 +                      SELECT COUNT(*) as cnt
       2347 +                      FROM v_struggle_priority
       2348 +                      WHERE struggle_weight >= 0.5
       2349 +                      AND atom_type IN ('mcq', 'true_false', 'parsons', 'matching')
       2350 +                      LIMIT 20
       2351 +                  ),
       2352 +                  due_atoms AS (
       2353 +                      SELECT COUNT(*) as cnt
       2354 +                      FROM learning_atoms
       2355 +                      WHERE anki_due_date IS NOT NULL
       2356 +                      AND anki_due_date <= CURRENT_DATE
       2357 +                      AND atom_type IN ('mcq', 'true_false', 'parsons', 'matching')
       2358 +                  ),
       2359 +                  new_atoms AS (
       2360 +                      SELECT COUNT(*) as cnt
       2361 +                      FROM learning_atoms
       2362 +                      WHERE (anki_review_count IS NULL OR anki_review_count = 0)
       2363 +                      AND atom_type IN ('mcq', 'true_false', 'parsons', 'matching')
       2364 +                  )
       2365 +                  SELECT
       2366 +                      (SELECT cnt FROM struggle_atoms) as struggle_count,
       2367 +                      (SELECT cnt FROM due_atoms) as due_count,
       2368 +                      (SELECT cnt FROM new_atoms) as new_count
       2369 +              """)
       2370 +          )
       2371 +          session_row = session_result.fetchone()
       2372 +
       2373 +          return {
       2374 +              "overall_mastery": float(mastery_row.overall_mastery or 0),
       2375 +              "sections_total": mastery_row.sections_total or 0,
       2376 +              "sections_complete": mastery_row.sections_complete or 0,
       2377 +              "streak_days": streak_row.streak or 0,
       2378 +              "struggle_zones": struggle_zones,
       2379 +              "struggle_count": session_row.struggle_count or 0,
       2380 +              "due_count": session_row.due_count or 0,
       2381 +              "new_count": session_row.new_count or 0,
       2382 +          }
       2383 +

       224 +  def _ensure_struggles_imported() -> bool:
       225 +      """Check if struggles are imported, auto-import if struggles.yaml exists and DB is empty."""
       226 +      try:
       227 +          with engine.connect() as conn:
       228 +              result = conn.execute(text("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM struggle_weights"))
       229 +              count = result.scalar() or 0
       230 +              if count > 0:
       231 +                  return True  # Already imported
       232 +
       233 +          # Check if struggles.yaml exists
       234 +          project_root = Path(__file__).parent.parent.parent
       235 +          yaml_path = project_root / "struggles.yaml"
       236 +          if yaml_path.exists():
       237 +              console.print("[dim]Auto-importing struggles from struggles.yaml...[/dim]")
       238 +              result = _import_struggles_to_db()
       239 +              console.print(f"[green][OK][/green] Imported {result['imported']} struggle weights\n")
       240 +              return True
       241 +          return False
       242 +      except Exception:
       243 +          return False  # Table might not exist
       244 +

â— All done! Here's a summary of what was implemented:

  Summary: Cortex Start UX Improvements

  Changes Made:

  1. src/cli/cortex.py
  - Added struggles command to import struggles.yaml â†’ struggle_weights table
  - Added _load_struggles_yaml(), _import_struggles_to_db(), _get_struggle_stats() helper functions
  - Added _get_pre_session_stats() to gather dashboard data from DB
  - Added _show_pre_session_dashboard() to display progress + struggle zones before session
  - Added _ensure_struggles_imported() for auto-import on first run
  - Modified cortex_start() to:
    - Auto-import struggles if DB is empty
    - Show pre-session dashboard with progress and struggle zones
    - Added --skip-dashboard option

  2. src/study/study_service.py
  - Modified get_adaptive_session() to:
    - Accept new use_struggles=True parameter
    - Query v_struggle_priority view for struggle-weighted atoms first
    - Fill remaining slots with FSRS due and new atoms
    - Log breakdown of atom sources (struggle, due, new)

  New Commands:

  nls cortex struggles              # Show struggle weights heatmap
  nls cortex struggles --import     # Import from struggles.yaml
  nls cortex start                  # Shows dashboard, then starts session
  nls cortex start --skip-dashboard # Skip the dashboard

  New UX Flow:

  1. cortex start auto-imports struggles.yaml if DB is empty
  2. Shows pre-session dashboard with:
    - Overall mastery percentage
    - Study streak
    - Top struggle zones (Module 5, 8, 9, etc. from your YAML)
    - Session composition preview (X from struggles, Y due, Z new)
  3. Prompts "INITIALIZE SESSION?" before starting
  4. Session prioritizes atoms from your declared struggle zones

       381 +                  table.add_column("Severity", justify="center")
       382 +                  table.add_column("Weight", justify="right")
       383 +                  table.add_column("Mastery", justify="right")
       384 +                  table.add_column("Notes", max_width=40)
       385 +
       386 +                  severity_colors = {
       387 +                      "critical": CORTEX_THEME["error"],
       388 +                      "high": CORTEX_THEME["warning"],
       389 +                      "medium": CORTEX_THEME["accent"],
       390 +                      "low": CORTEX_THEME["dim"],
       391 +                  }
       392 +
       393 +                  for s in struggles:
       394 +                      severity_style = Style(color=severity_colors.get(s["severity"], CORTEX_THEME["dim"]))
       395 +                      mastery_pct = s["avg_mastery"]
       396 +                      mastery_style = Style(
       397 +                          color=CORTEX_THEME["success"] if mastery_pct >= 70 else (
       398 +                              CORTEX_THEME["warning"] if mastery_pct >= 40 else CORTEX_THEME["error"]
       399 +                          )
       400 +                      )
       401 +                      table.add_row(
       402 +                          f"M{s['module_number']:02d}",
       403 +                          Text(s["severity"].upper(), style=severity_style),
       404 +                          f"{s['weight']:.2f}",
       405 +                          Text(f"{mastery_pct:.0f}%", style=mastery_style),
       406 +                          s["notes"][:40] if s["notes"] else "",
       407 +                      )
       408 +                  console.print(table)
       409 +              else:
       410 +                  console.print("[yellow]No struggles configured. Select option 4 to import.[/yellow]")
       411 +
       412 +              console.print("\n[dim]Press Enter to return to hub...[/dim]")
       413 +              input()
       414 +
       415 +          elif choice == "4":
       416 +              # Import struggles
       417 +              console.print("\n[cyan]Importing struggles from struggles.yaml...[/cyan]")
       418 +              result = _import_struggles_to_db()
       419 +              if result.get("errors"):
       420 +                  for err in result["errors"]:
       421 +                      console.print(f"[yellow]Warning: {err}[/yellow]")
       422 +              console.print(f"[green][OK][/green] Imported {result['imported']} struggle weights")
       423 +              console.print("\n[dim]Press Enter to return to hub...[/dim]")
       424 +              input()
       425 +
       426 +          elif choice == "5":
       427 +              # Configure modules
       428 +              console.print("\n[bold cyan]MODULE CONFIGURATION[/bold cyan]\n")
       429 +              console.print("[dim]Available modules: 1-17[/dim]")
       430 +              console.print("  [cyan]1-10[/cyan]: Fundamentals (OSI, TCP/IP, Addressing)")
       431 +              console.print("  [cyan]11-17[/cyan]: Advanced (Routing, Switching, Security)")
       432 +              console.print()
       433 +              console.print(f"[dim]Current selection: {module_list}[/dim]\n")
       434 +
       435 +              modules_input = Prompt.ask(
       436 +                  "[cyan]>_ MODULES (e.g., 1-17 or 5,8,9)[/cyan]",
       437 +                  default=",".join(str(m) for m in module_list),
       438 +              )
       439 +
       440 +              # Parse range notation
       441 +              new_modules = []
       442 +              for part in modules_input.split(","):
       443 +                  part = part.strip()
       444 +                  if "-" in part:
       445 +                      try:
       446 +                          start_m, end_m = part.split("-")
       447 +                          new_modules.extend(range(int(start_m), int(end_m) + 1))
       448 +                      except ValueError:
       449 +                          pass
       450 +                  elif part.isdigit():
       451 +                      new_modules.append(int(part))
       452 +
       453 +              if new_modules:
       454 +                  module_list = sorted(set(new_modules))
       455 +                  console.print(f"[green][OK][/green] Modules set to: {module_list}")
       456 +              else:
       457 +                  console.print("[yellow]Invalid input, keeping current selection[/yellow]")
       458 +
       459 +              # Also configure limit
       460 +              limit_input = Prompt.ask(
       461 +                  "[cyan]>_ ATOMS PER SESSION[/cyan]",
       462 +                  default=str(limit),
       463 +              )
       464 +              if limit_input.isdigit():
       465 +                  limit = int(limit_input)
       466 +                  console.print(f"[green][OK][/green] Limit set to: {limit}")
       467 +
       468 +              console.print("\n[dim]Press Enter to return to hub...[/dim]")
       469 +              input()
       470 +
       471 +          elif choice == "6":
       472 +              # Resume session
       473 +              session = CortexSession.resume_latest()
       474 +              if session:
       475 +                  state = session._session_state
       476 +                  console.print(
       477 +                      Panel(
       478 +                          f"[cyan]Found saved session[/cyan]\n\n"
       479 +                          f"Mode: [bold]{state.mode.upper()}[/bold]\n"
       480 +                          f"Started: {state.started_at[:19]}\n"
       481 +                          f"Progress: {state.correct + state.incorrect} completed, "
       482 +                          f"{len(state.atoms_remaining)} remaining\n"
       483 +                          f"Score: {state.correct} correct, {state.incorrect} incorrect",
       484 +                          border_style=Style(color=CORTEX_THEME["accent"]),
       485 +                          box=box.ROUNDED,
       486 +                      )
       487 +                  )
       488 +                  if Confirm.ask("Resume this session?", default=True):
       489 +                      session.run()
       490 +              else:
       491 +                  console.print("[yellow]No saved session found.[/yellow]")
       492 +
       493 +              console.print("\n[dim]Press Enter to return to hub...[/dim]")
       494 +              input()
       495 +
       496 +          elif choice == "q":
       497 +              console.print("\n[dim]Exiting Cortex...[/dim]")
       498 +              break
       499 +
       500 +
       501 +  @cortex_app.command("start")
       502 +  def cortex_start(
       503 +      limit: int = typer.Option(20, help="Atoms per session"),
       504 +      quick: bool = typer.Option(
       505 +          False,
       506 +          "--quick", "-q",
       507 +          help="Skip hub, start adaptive session immediately",
       508 +      ),
       509 +  ):
       510 +      """
       511 +      Launch the Cortex study hub.
       512 +
       513 +      The hub shows your progress, struggle zones, and lets you:
       514 +      - Start adaptive or war mode sessions
       515 +      - View and manage struggle weights
       516 +      - Configure modules and session size
       517 +      - Resume previous sessions
       518 +
       519 +      Use --quick to skip the hub and start immediately.
       520 +
       521 +      Examples:
       522 +          nls cortex start           # Open interactive hub
       523 +          nls cortex start --quick   # Start session immediately
       524 +      """
       525 +      if quick:
       526 +          # Quick mode: skip hub, start adaptive session immediately
       527 +          _ensure_struggles_imported()
       528 +          module_list = list(range(1, 18))
       529 +          session = CortexSession(modules=module_list, limit=limit, war_mode=False)
       530 +          session.run()
       531 +      else:
       532 +          # Interactive hub
       533 +          _run_interactive_hub(initial_limit=limit)
       534 +
       535 +
       536    @cortex_app.command("war")
       537    def cortex_war(
       538        limit: int = typer.Option(25, help="Notes to pull into the cram deck"),
       539    ):
       540 -      """Alias for war mode."""
       540 +      """Quick war mode (cram) session - skips hub."""

       543        session = CortexSession(modules=module_list, limit=limit, war_mode=True)
       544        session.run()

  - nls cortex war - Skip hub, start war mode immediately

     Plan: Cortex Session UX & Remediation Fixes

     Completed (Previous Session)

     - Interactive hub with dashboard, struggles, module config
     - get_adaptive_session() uses v_struggle_priority view
     - Auto-import from struggles.yaml

     New Issues from Testing

     User tested cortex start and found:

     Issue 1: False Fatigue Detection (CRITICAL)

     After only 3 correct answers (38 seconds), system triggers "COGNITIVE FATIGUE" micro-break.
     - Root cause: FatigueVector.is_critical threshold is 0.7 norm, but 3D Euclidean norm reaches this too quickly
     - Location: src/adaptive/ncde_pipeline.py:138-140

     Issue 2: No Re-Teaching After Errors

     When user got port-security question wrong, system just moved on.
     - Expected: Re-teach concept, show similar questions, or explain error
     - The remediation infrastructure exists (ForceZStrategy, PLMStrategy) but isn't being triggered properly

     Issue 3: Debug Logs Visible

     2025-12-12 17:47:49.562 | DEBUG | src.adaptive.ncde_pipeline... showing in session

     Issue 4: No Anki Filtered Deck Suggestions

     After session, no recommendation for what to study in Anki

     Implementation Plan

     Fix 1: Fatigue Detection Too Sensitive

     File: src/adaptive/ncde_pipeline.py

     Current problem:
     # Line 138-140
     @property
     def is_critical(self) -> bool:
         return self.norm > 0.7  # Too low!

     Solution: Add minimum session time/interactions before fatigue can trigger:
     @property
     def is_critical(self) -> bool:
         """Fatigue only triggers after meaningful session duration."""
         return self.norm > 0.85  # Raise threshold

     # In RemediationSelector.select():
     def select(self, diagnosis, fatigue, psi, confusion_matrix, target_concept, session_context):
         # Only check fatigue after 10+ interactions or 10+ minutes
         if session_context.interaction_count >= 10 or session_context.elapsed_minutes >= 10:
             if fatigue.is_critical:
                 return MicroBreakStrategy(break_minutes=10)
         # ... rest of logic

     Fix 2: Immediate Retry on Errors

     File: src/cortex/session.py

     Current: After incorrect answer, just shows diagnosis panel and moves on.

     Solution: Immediate retry with hint, then show answer if still wrong:
     # After incorrect answer:
     if not is_correct:
         # First attempt wrong â†’ show hint and retry immediately
         if not atom.get("_retried"):
             console.print("[yellow]Incorrect. Here's a hint:[/yellow]")
             hint = self._generate_hint(atom)  # e.g., "Think about mode hierarchy"
             console.print(f"[cyan]{hint}[/cyan]")
             console.print("\n[dim]Try again...[/dim]\n")

             atom["_retried"] = True
             # Re-present same question (don't advance index)
             continue  # Loop will re-show this atom

         else:
             # Second attempt also wrong â†’ show correct answer
             console.print(f"[red]Incorrect.[/red] The answer was:")
             console.print(f"[green]{correct_answer}[/green]")
             self._display_diagnosis(diagnosis)
             # Track for Anki suggestions
             self._incorrect_atoms.append(atom)

     Hint generation (for Parsons questions):
     def _generate_hint(self, atom: dict) -> str:
         """Generate a contextual hint based on atom type."""
         atom_type = atom.get("atom_type")

         if atom_type == "parsons":
             # Hint: first step
             steps = atom.get("_steps", [])
             if steps:
                 return f"Start with: {steps[0]}"

         elif atom_type == "mcq":
             # Hint: eliminate one wrong answer
             return "Eliminate options that don't match the context..."

         return "Review the question carefully."

     Fix 3: Hide Debug Logs

     File: config.py or logging config

     # Set loguru to INFO level for production
     import sys
     from loguru import logger
     logger.remove()
     logger.add(sys.stderr, level="INFO")  # Not DEBUG

     Or in cortex session startup:
     import logging
     logging.getLogger("src.adaptive").setLevel(logging.WARNING)

     Fix 4: Anki Filtered Deck Suggestions

     File: src/cortex/session.py (add to session summary)

     After session ends, show:
     SESSION COMPLETE
     ================
     Correct: 15/20 (75%)
     Struggled sections: 2.3, 5.1, 7.2

     ANKI STUDY SUGGESTIONS
     ======================
     Copy these filtered deck queries:

     1. High priority (sections you struggled):
        deck:CCNA::ITN::* (tag:section:2.3 OR tag:section:5.1 OR tag:section:7.2)

     2. Review atoms from this session:
        deck:CCNA::ITN::* rated:1:1  (cards rated "again" today)

     Implementation:
     def _show_session_summary(self):
         # ... existing summary ...

         # Collect struggled sections
         struggled = [a["section_id"] for a in self._incorrect_atoms]
         unique_sections = list(set(struggled))

         if unique_sections:
             tags = " OR ".join(f"tag:section:{s}" for s in unique_sections[:5])
             anki_query = f"deck:CCNA::ITN::* ({tags})"

             console.print("\n[bold cyan]ANKI STUDY SUGGESTION[/bold cyan]")
             console.print(f"Filtered deck query for struggled sections:")
             console.print(f"[yellow]{anki_query}[/yellow]")

       686 +      def _generate_hint(self, atom: dict) -> str:
       687 +          """
       688 +          Generate a contextual hint for an atom based on its type.
       689 +
       690 +          Evidence-based: Hints provide scaffolding without giving away the answer.
       691 +          """
       692 +          atom_type = atom.get("atom_type", "")
       693 +
       694 +          if atom_type == "parsons":
       695 +              # Hint: show first step
       696 +              steps = atom.get("_steps", [])
       697 +              if steps:
       698 +                  return f"Start with: {steps[0]}"
       699 +              return "Think about the logical order of operations."
       700 +
       701 +          elif atom_type == "mcq":
       702 +              # Hint: eliminate most obviously wrong option
       703 +              options = atom.get("options", [])
       704 +              correct = atom.get("correct_answer", "")
       705 +              if options and len(options) > 2:
       706 +                  # Find obviously wrong answer (often the shortest or most generic)
       707 +                  for opt in options:
       708 +                      if opt != correct and len(opt) < 5:
       709 +                          return f"Eliminate: \"{opt}\" is likely incorrect."
       710 +              return "Read each option carefully. One stands out as correct."
       711 +
       712 +          elif atom_type == "true_false":
       713 +              front = atom.get("front", "")
       714 +              # Look for absolute words that are often false
       715 +              absolutes = ["always", "never", "all", "none", "only"]
       716 +              if any(word in front.lower() for word in absolutes):
       717 +                  return "Watch out for absolute words like 'always' or 'never'."
       718 +              return "Consider: Is this statement universally true?"
       719 +
       720 +          elif atom_type == "matching":
       721 +              pairs = atom.get("pairs", [])
       722 +              if pairs:
       723 +                  # Show one free match
       724 +                  first = pairs[0]
       725 +                  return f"One match: {first[0]} â†’ {first[1]}"
       726 +              return "Match items that belong together conceptually."
       727 +
       728 +          elif atom_type == "numeric":
       729 +              answer = atom.get("back", "")
       730 +              if answer:
       731 +                  # Show magnitude hint
       732 +                  try:
       733 +                      num = float(answer.split()[0])
       734 +                      if num < 10:
       735 +                          return "The answer is a small number (< 10)."
       736 +                      elif num < 100:
       737 +                          return "The answer is between 10 and 100."
       738 +                      else:
       739 +                          return f"The answer is larger than 100."
       740 +                  except (ValueError, IndexError):
       741 +                      pass
       742 +              return "Double-check your units and calculations."
       743 +
       744 +          # Default hint
       745 +          return "Read the question carefully and think step-by-step."
       746 +

       754 +

       760 +              else:

       880 +      def _display_anki_suggestions(self) -> None:
       881 +          """
       882 +          Display Anki filtered deck suggestions based on struggled sections.
       883 +
       884 +          Tag format: tag:section:X.Y.Z (verified against Anki deck structure)
       885 +          Deck: CCNA::ITN::*
       886 +          """
       887 +          # Extract unique section IDs from incorrect atoms
       888 +          struggled_sections: set[str] = set()
       889 +          for atom in self._incorrect_atoms:
       890 +              # Try multiple sources for section_id
       891 +              section_id = atom.get("section_id")
       892 +              if not section_id:
       893 +                  # Try to extract from tags or other fields
       894 +                  tags = atom.get("tags", [])
       895 +                  for tag in tags:
       896 +                      if tag.startswith("section:"):
       897 +                          section_id = tag.replace("section:", "")
       898 +                          break
       899 +              if not section_id:
       900 +                  # Try source_section field
       901 +                  section_id = atom.get("source_section")
       902 +              if section_id:
       903 +                  struggled_sections.add(str(section_id))
       904 +
       905 +          if not struggled_sections:
       906 +              # No section info available
       907 +              console.print(Panel(
       908 +                  "[dim]No section data available for Anki suggestions.[/dim]",
       909 +                  border_style=Style(color=CORTEX_THEME["dim"]),
       910 +                  box=box.ROUNDED,
       911 +              ))
       912 +              return
       913 +
       914 +          # Build Anki filtered deck query
       915 +          # Format: deck:CCNA::ITN::* (tag:section:X.Y OR tag:section:X.Z)
       916 +          section_tags = [f"tag:section:{s}" for s in sorted(struggled_sections)]
       917 +
       918 +          # Build the query string
       919 +          if len(section_tags) == 1:
       920 +              tag_clause = section_tags[0]
       921 +          else:
       922 +              tag_clause = "(" + " OR ".join(section_tags) + ")"
       923 +
       924 +          anki_query = f"deck:CCNA::ITN::* {tag_clause} -is:suspended"
       925 +
       926 +          # Create display panel
       927 +          anki_text = Text()
       928 +          anki_text.append("ğŸ“š ANKI STUDY SUGGESTION\n\n", style=Style(color=CORTEX_THEME["accent"], bold=True))
       929 +          anki_text.append("You struggled with ", style=STYLES["cortex_dim"])
       930 +          anki_text.append(f"{len(struggled_sections)} section(s)", style=Style(color=CORTEX_THEME["warning"]))
       931 +          anki_text.append(". Use this filtered deck query:\n\n", style=STYLES["cortex_dim"])
       932 +
       933 +          # Display query in copyable format
       934 +          anki_text.append(anki_query, style=Style(color=CORTEX_THEME["success"]))
       935 +          anki_text.append("\n\n", style=STYLES["cortex_dim"])
       936 +
       937 +          # Show individual sections
       938 +          anki_text.append("Sections to review:\n", style=STYLES["cortex_dim"])
       939 +          for section in sorted(struggled_sections)[:10]:  # Limit to 10
       940 +              anki_text.append(f"  â€¢ {section}\n", style=Style(color=CORTEX_THEME["secondary"]))
       941 +
       942 +          if len(struggled_sections) > 10:
       943 +              anki_text.append(f"  ... and {len(struggled_sections) - 10} more\n", style=STYLES["cortex_dim"])
       944 +
       945 +          # How to use
       946 +          anki_text.append("\n[Instructions: Anki â†’ Tools â†’ Create Filtered Deck â†’ paste query]", style=STYLES["cortex_dim"])
       947 +
       948 +          console.print(Panel(
       949 +              anki_text,
       950 +              border_style=Style(color=CORTEX_THEME["accent"]),
       951 +              box=box.ROUNDED,

        961 +      def _offer_llm_generation(self) -> None:
        962 +          """
        963 +          Offer to generate additional LLM-based practice content for weak areas.
        964 +
        965 +          Uses existing LLM generator infrastructure to create supplementary atoms.
        966 +          """
        967 +          if not self._incorrect_atoms:
        968 +              return
        969 +
        970 +          # Ask user if they want to generate more content
        971 +          console.print()
        972 +          generate = Confirm.ask(
        973 +              "[cyan]Generate additional practice questions for struggled areas?[/cyan]",
        974 +              default=False
        975 +          )
        976 +
        977 +          if not generate:
        978 +              return
        979 +
        980 +          # Get unique sections from incorrect atoms
        981 +          weak_sections = set()
        982 +          for atom in self._incorrect_atoms:
        983 +              section_id = atom.get("section_id") or atom.get("source_section")
        984 +              if section_id:
        985 +                  weak_sections.add(str(section_id))
        986 +
        987 +          if not weak_sections:
        988 +              console.print("[dim]No section data available for content generation.[/dim]")
        989 +              return
        990 +
        991 +          with CortexSpinner(console, "Generating practice content via LLM..."):
        992 +              try:
        993 +                  from src.content.generation.llm_generator import LLMFlashcardGenerator
        994 +
        995 +                  generator = LLMFlashcardGenerator(use_quality_validation=False)
        996 +
        997 +                  # Generate additional atoms for each weak section
        998 +                  generated_count = 0
        999 +                  for section_id in list(weak_sections)[:3]:  # Limit to 3 sections
       1000 +                      # Find source content for this section
       1001 +                      source_atom = next(
       1002 +                          (a for a in self._incorrect_atoms
       1003 +                           if str(a.get("section_id") or a.get("source_section")) == section_id),
       1004 +                          None
       1005 +                      )
       1006 +
       1007 +                      if source_atom:
       1008 +                          # Use the atom's context for generation
       1009 +                          source_text = source_atom.get("source_fact_basis", "")
       1010 +                          if not source_text:
       1011 +                              source_text = f"{source_atom.get('front', '')} {source_atom.get('back', '')}"
       1012 +
       1013 +                          cards = generator.generate_from_text(
       1014 +                              text=source_text,
       1015 +                              section_id=section_id,
       1016 +                              module_number=int(section_id.split(".")[0]) if "." in section_id else 1,
       1017 +                              max_cards=3,
       1018 +                          )
       1019 +                          generated_count += len(cards)
       1020 +
       1021 +                  if generated_count > 0:
       1022 +                      gen_text = Text()
       1023 +                      gen_text.append(f"âœ“ Generated {generated_count} practice questions\n\n", style=STYLES["cortex_success"])
       1024 +                      gen_text.append("New questions have been added to the database.\n", style=STYLES["cortex_dim"])
       1025 +                      gen_text.append("Run another session to practice them!", style=Style(color=CORTEX_THEME["accent"]))
       1026 +
       1027 +                      console.print(Panel(
       1028 +                          gen_text,
       1029 +                          border_style=Style(color=CORTEX_THEME["success"]),
       1030 +                          box=box.ROUNDED,
       1031 +                          padding=(0, 1),
       1032 +                      ))
       1033 +                  else:
       1034 +                      console.print("[dim]No additional content could be generated.[/dim]")
       1035 +

  Summary of Fixes Implemented

  1. Fatigue Detection False Positives (Fixed)

  File: src/adaptive/ncde_pipeline.py

  - Added minimum session requirements before fatigue can trigger:
    - Must have 10+ interactions OR 10+ minutes elapsed
    - Added session_context parameter to RemediationSelector.select()

  2. Debug Logs Hidden (Fixed)

  File: src/cortex/session.py
  - Added loguru configuration at module level to set log level to INFO
  - Format: <dim>{time:HH:mm:ss}</dim> | <level>{level: <8}</level> | {message}

  3. Immediate Retry on Errors with Hints (Implemented)

  File: src/cortex/session.py
  - Added _incorrect_atoms list to track atoms for Anki suggestions
  - Added _generate_hint() method with type-specific hints:
    - Parsons: Shows first step
    - MCQ: Elimination hints
    - True/False: Warns about absolute words
    - Matching: Shows one free match
    - Numeric: Gives magnitude range
  - Added _show_correct_answer() method
  - Modified run loop:
    - First wrong: Show hint, retry same question
    - Second wrong: Show correct answer, track for Anki

  4. Anki Filtered Deck Suggestions (Implemented)

  File: src/cortex/session.py
  - Added _display_anki_suggestions() method
  - Extracts section IDs from incorrect atoms
  - Generates valid Anki filtered deck query:
    - Format: deck:CCNA::ITN::* (tag:section:X.Y OR tag:section:X.Z) -is:suspended
  - Shows sections to review and usage instructions

  5. LLM Content Generation for Weak Areas (Implemented)

  File: src/cortex/session.py
  - Added _offer_llm_generation() method
  - Prompts user after session if they want more practice content
  - Uses existing LLMFlashcardGenerator infrastructure
  - Generates up to 3 questions per weak section (max 3 sections)

  File: src/cli/cortex.py

â— Now I understand the problem clearly. The FatigueVectorCalculator has _history and _rt_history lists that accumulate data. When you take a micro-break,
  the session resets session_context.fatigue to a new FatigueVector(), but the calculator's history is not cleared. So the next call to calculate() will
  immediately produce another high fatigue value from the old data.

  The calculator needs a reset() method, and that needs to be called from NCDEPipeline when we want to reset after a break.

     Plan: Cortex Session Critical Fixes (Round 2)

     Completed in Previous Implementation

     - Raised fatigue threshold from 0.7 to 0.85
     - Added min interactions check (10+ interactions OR 10+ minutes)
     - Added immediate retry on errors with hints
     - Added Anki filtered deck suggestions
     - Added LLM content generation offer
     - Configured loguru to INFO level (but not working)
     - Redesigned UI panels (Score, Brain State) - NOT BEING USED

     NEW CRITICAL BUGS FROM TESTING

     User ran cortex start and discovered:

     Issue 1: Fatigue Not Resetting After Micro-Break (CRITICAL)

     Symptom: After taking a micro-break, fatigue immediately goes back to 100% and triggers another break on the next question.
     Root Cause: session.py:531 resets session_context.fatigue = FatigueVector(), but the FatigueVectorCalculator in ncde_pipeline.py keeps its internal
     _history and _rt_history lists, so calculate() immediately produces high fatigue again.
     Evidence: In logs: RemediationSelector: Fatigue critical (1.00) fires after EVERY correct answer

     Issue 2: INFO Logs Still Showing

     Symptom: 18:17:05 | INFO | NCDE: Diagnosis complete... still visible during session
     Root Cause: The loguru config in session.py:19-27 sets INFO level, but NCDE pipeline uses logger.info() which still shows INFO logs. Need WARNING
     level.

     Issue 3: Old UI Layout Still Being Used

     Symptom: Still showing "TELEMETRY" panel with PROCESSED/CORRECT/ERRORS and old "NEURO-LINK [NOMINAL]" panel with ENCODING/INTEGRATION/FOCUS/FATIGUE
     at 100%
     Root Cause: The new _stats_panel(), _neurolink_panel(), and _layout() methods were added but might not be getting called, OR there's another file
     rendering the old UI

     Issue 4: Parsons Questions May Have Incomplete Steps

     Symptom: Some Parsons only show 2 steps when the task requires more
     Root Cause: Data quality issue - atoms in database have incomplete back fields

     Implementation Plan

     Fix 1: Fatigue Calculator Reset Method

     File: src/adaptive/ncde_pipeline.py

     Add reset method to FatigueVectorCalculator:
     class FatigueVectorCalculator:
         # ... existing code ...

         def reset(self) -> None:
             """Clear history after a micro-break to reset fatigue calculation."""
             self._history = []
             self._rt_history = []

     Add reset method to NCDEPipeline:
     class NCDEPipeline:
         def reset_fatigue(self) -> None:
             """Reset fatigue calculator after a micro-break."""
             self.fatigue_calculator.reset()

     File: src/cortex/session.py

     Update micro-break handler:
     if strategy.name == "micro_break":
         self._trigger_micro_break(strategy)
         # Reset fatigue in BOTH places
         self.session_context.fatigue = FatigueVector()
         self.ncde.reset_fatigue()  # NEW: Clear calculator history

     Fix 2: Set Log Level to WARNING

     File: src/cortex/session.py

     Change line 25:
     # FROM:
     loguru_logger.add(sys.stderr, level="INFO", ...)
     # TO:
     loguru_logger.add(sys.stderr, level="WARNING", ...)
